<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span>npm install zod@^4.0.0</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<!-- -->
<p>Many of Zod&#x27;s behaviors and APIs have been made more intuitive and cohesive. The breaking changes described in this document often represent major quality-of-life improvements for Zod users. I strongly recommend reading this guide thoroughly.</p>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin"><p><strong>Note</strong> — Zod 3 exported a number of undocumented quasi-internal utility types and functions that are not considered part of the public API. Changes to those are not documented here.</p></div></div></div>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin"><p><strong>Unofficial codemod</strong> — A community-maintained codemod <a href="https://github.com/nicoespeon/zod-v3-to-v4" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank"><code>zod-v3-to-v4</code></a> is available.</p></div></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="error-customization"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=error-customization">Error customization</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Zod 4 standardizes the APIs for error customization under a single, unified <code>error</code> param. Previously Zod&#x27;s error customization APIs were fragmented and inconsistent. This is cleaned up in Zod 4.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="deprecates-message-parameter"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=deprecates-message-parameter">deprecates <code>message</code> parameter</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Replaces <code>message</code> param with <code>error</code>. The old <code>message</code> parameter is still supported but deprecated.</p>

[@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 short.&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> });</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:rounded-none [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:border-none"></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-invalid_type_error-and-required_error"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-invalid_type_error-and-required_error">drops <code>invalid_type_error</code> and <code>required_error</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>invalid_type_error</code> / <code>required_error</code> params have been dropped. These were hastily added years ago as a way to customize errors that was less verbose than <code>errorMap</code>. They came with all sorts of footguns (they can&#x27;t be used in conjunction with <code>errorMap</code>) and do not align with Zod&#x27;s actual issue codes (there is no <code>required</code> issue code).</p>
<p>These can now be cleanly represented with the new <code>error</code> parameter.</p>
<div dir="ltr" data-orientation="horizontal" class="flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-xl border bg-fd-card my-4"><div role="tablist" aria-orientation="horizontal" class="flex flex-row items-end data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">  error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">issue</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> issue.input </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">===</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    ?</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;This field is required&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    :</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;Not a string&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_tiilubv9fl5b_-trigger-zod-3" hidden="" id="radix-_R_tiilubv9fl5b_-content-zod-3" tabindex="0" class="p-4 prose-no-margin [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:-m-4 [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:rounded-none [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:border-none"></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-errormap"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-errormap">drops <code>errorMap</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This is renamed to <code>error</code>.</p>
<p>Error maps can also now return a plain <code>string</code> (instead of <code>{message: string}</code>). They can also return <code>undefined</code>, which tells Zod to yield control to the next error map in the chain.</p>

<p>The issue formats have been dramatically streamlined.</p>

<p>Below is the list of Zod 3 issues types and their Zod 4 equivalent:</p>

<p>While certain Zod 4 issue types have been merged, dropped, and modified, each issue remains structurally similar to Zod 3 counterpart (identical, in most cases). All issues still conform to the same base interface as Zod 3, so most common error handling logic will work without modification.</p>

<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="changes-error-map-precedence"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=changes-error-map-precedence">changes error map precedence</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The error map precedence has been changed to be more consistent. Specifically, an error map passed into <code>.parse()</code> <em>no longer</em> takes precedence over a schema-level error map.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 <h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="deprecates-format"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=deprecates-format">deprecates <code>.format()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>.format()</code> method on <code>ZodError</code> has been deprecated. Instead use the top-level <code>z.treeifyError()</code> function. Read the <a href="/error-formatting">Formatting errors docs</a> for more information.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="deprecates-flatten"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=deprecates-flatten">deprecates <code>.flatten()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>.flatten()</code> method on <code>ZodError</code> has also been deprecated. Instead use the top-level <code>z.treeifyError()</code> function. Read the <a href="/error-formatting">Formatting errors docs</a> for more information.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-formerrors"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-formerrors">drops <code>.formErrors</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This API was identical to <code>.flatten()</code>. It exists for historical reasons and isn&#x27;t documented.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="deprecates-addissue-and-addissues"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=deprecates-addissue-and-addissues">deprecates <code>.addIssue()</code> and <code>.addIssues()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Directly push to <code>err.issues</code> array instead, if necessary.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" <!-- -->
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="znumber"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=znumber"><code>z.number()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="no-infinite-values"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=no-infinite-values">no infinite values</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p><code>POSITIVE_INFINITY</code> and <code>NEGATIVE_INFINITY</code> are no longer considered valid values for <code>z.number()</code>.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="safe-no-longer-accepts-floats"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=safe-no-longer-accepts-floats"><code>.safe()</code> no longer accepts floats</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>In Zod 3, <code>z.number().safe()</code> is deprecated. It now behaves identically to <code>.int()</code> (see below). Importantly, that means it no longer accepts floats.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="int-accepts-safe-integers-only"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=int-accepts-safe-integers-only"><code>.int()</code> accepts safe integers only</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>z.number().int()</code> API no longer accepts unsafe integers (outside the range of <code>Number.MIN_SAFE_INTEGER</code> and <code>Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER</code>). Using integers out of this range causes spontaneous rounding errors. (Also: You should switch to <code>z.int()</code>.)</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zstring-updates"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zstring-updates"><code>z.string()</code> updates</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="deprecates-email-etc"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=deprecates-email-etc">deprecates <code>.email()</code> etc</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>String formats are now represented as <em>subclasses</em> of <code>ZodString</code>, instead of simple internal refinements. As such, these APIs have been moved to the top-level <code>z</code> namespace. Top-level APIs are also less verbose and more tree-shakable.</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">cidrv4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();          </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ip range</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">cidrv6</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();          </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ip range</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">time</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">datetime</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.iso.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">duration</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>The method forms (<code>z.string().email()</code>) still exist and work as before, but are now deprecated.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ deprecated</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ </span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="stricter-uuid"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=stricter-uuid">stricter <code>.uuid()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>z.uuid()</code> now validates UUIDs more strictly against the RFC 9562/4122 specification; specifically, the variant bits must be <code>10</code> per the spec. For a more permissive &quot;UUID-like&quot; validator, use <code>z.guid()</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">uuid</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// RFC 9562/4122 compliant UUID</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">guid</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// any 8-4-4-4-12 hex pattern</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="no-padding-in-base64url"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=no-padding-in-base64url">no padding in <code>.base64url()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Padding is no longer allowed in <code>z.base64url()</code> (formerly <code>z.string().base64url()</code>). Generally it&#x27;s desirable for base64url strings to be unpadded and URL-safe.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-zstringip"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-zstringip">drops <code>z.string().ip()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This has been replaced with separate <code>.ipv4()</code> and <code>.ipv6()</code> methods. Use <code>z.union()</code> to combine them if you need to accept both.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">ipv4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">ipv6</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="updates-zstringipv6"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=updates-zstringipv6">updates <code>z.string().ipv6()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Validation now happens using the <code>new URL()</code> constructor, which is far more robust than the old regular expression approach. Some invalid values that passed validation previously may now fail.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-zstringcidr"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-zstringcidr">drops <code>z.string().cidr()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Similarly, this has been replaced with separate <code>.cidrv4()</code> and <code>.cidrv6()</code> methods. Use <code>z.union()</code> to combine them if you need to accept both.</p>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">cidrv6</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zcoerce-updates"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zcoerce-updates"><code>z.coerce</code> updates</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The input type of all <code>z.coerce</code> schemas is now <code>unknown</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span
