<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> schemaInput</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">typeof</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> schema&gt;;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3: string;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4: unknown;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="default-updates"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=default-updates"><code>.default()</code> updates</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The application of <code>.default()</code> has changed in a subtle way. If the input is <code>undefined</code>, <code>ZodDefault</code> short-circuits the parsing process and returns the default value. The default value must be assignable to the <em>output type</em>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  .</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">transform</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">val</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> val.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  .</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// should be a number</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; 0</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>In Zod 3, <code>.default()</code> expected a value that matched the <em>input type</em>. <code>ZodDefault</code> would parse the default value, instead of short-circuiting. As such, the default value must be assignable to the <em>input type</em> of the schema.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  .</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">transform</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">val</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> val.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  .</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;tuna&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; 4</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>To replicate the old behavior, Zod implements a new <code>.prefault()</code> API. This is short for &quot;pre-parse default&quot;.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  .</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">transform</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">val</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> val.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  .</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">prefault</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;tuna&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">undefined</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; 4</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zobject"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zobject"><code>z.object()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="defaults-applied-within-optional-fields"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=defaults-applied-within-optional-fields">defaults applied within optional fields</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Defaults inside your properties are applied, even within optional fields. This aligns better with expectations and resolves a long-standing usability issue with Zod 3. This is a subtle change that may cause breakage in code paths that rely on key existence, etc.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  a: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;tuna&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">optional</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4: { a: &quot;tuna&quot; }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3: {}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="deprecates-strict-and-passthrough"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=deprecates-strict-and-passthrough">deprecates <code>.strict()</code> and <code>.passthrough()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>These methods are generally no longer necessary. Instead use the top-level <code>z.strictObject()</code> and <code>z.looseObject()</code> functions.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() }).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">strict</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() }).</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">passthrough</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">strictObject</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">looseObject</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() });</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p>These methods are still available for backwards compatibility, and they will not be removed. They are considered legacy.</p>
</div></div></div>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="deprecates-strip"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=deprecates-strip">deprecates <code>.strip()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This was never particularly useful, as it was the default behavior of <code>z.object()</code>. To convert a strict object to a &quot;regular&quot; one, use <code>z.object(A.shape)</code>.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-nonstrict"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-nonstrict">drops <code>.nonstrict()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This long-deprecated alias for <code>.strip()</code> has been removed.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-deeppartial"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-deeppartial">drops <code>.deepPartial()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This has been long deprecated in Zod 3 and it now removed in Zod 4. There is no direct alternative to this API. There were lots of footguns in its implementation, and its use is generally an anti-pattern.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="changes-zunknown-optionality"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=changes-zunknown-optionality">changes <code>z.unknown()</code> optionality</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>z.unknown()</code> and <code>z.any()</code> types are no longer marked as &quot;key optional&quot; in the inferred types.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> mySchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  a: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">any</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  b: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3: { a?: any; b?: unknown };</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4: { a: any; b: unknown };</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="deprecates-merge"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=deprecates-merge">deprecates <code>.merge()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>.merge()</code> method on <code>ZodObject</code> has been deprecated in favor of <code>.extend()</code>. The <code>.extend()</code> method provides the same functionality, avoids ambiguity around strictness inheritance, and has better TypeScript performance.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// .merge (deprecated)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> ExtendedSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> BaseSchema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">merge</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(AdditionalSchema);</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// .extend (recommended)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> ExtendedSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> BaseSchema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">extend</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(AdditionalSchema.shape);</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// or use destructuring (best tsc performance)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> ExtendedSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  ...</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">BaseSchema.shape,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  ...</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">AdditionalSchema.shape,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p><strong>Note</strong>: For even better TypeScript performance, consider using object destructuring instead of <code>.extend()</code>. See the <a href="/api?id=extend">API documentation</a> for more details.</p>
</div></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="znativeenum-deprecated"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=znativeenum-deprecated"><code>z.nativeEnum()</code> deprecated</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The <code>z.nativeEnum()</code> function is now deprecated in favor of just <code>z.enum()</code>. The <code>z.enum()</code> API has been overloaded to support an enum-like input.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">enum</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Color</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  Red</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;red&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  Green</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;green&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  Blue</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;blue&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> ColorSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">enum</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(Color); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>As part of this refactor of <code>ZodEnum</code>, a number of long-deprecated and redundant features have been removed. These were all identical and only existed for historical reasons.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">ColorSchema.enum.Red; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ =&gt; &quot;Red&quot; (canonical API)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">ColorSchema.Enum.Red; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ removed</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">ColorSchema.Values.Red; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ removed</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zarray"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zarray"><code>z.array()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="changes-nonempty-type"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=changes-nonempty-type">changes <code>.nonempty()</code> type</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This now behaves identically to <code>z.array().min(1)</code>. The inferred type does not change.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> NonEmpty</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">array</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">nonempty</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> NonEmpty</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">infer</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">typeof</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NonEmpty&gt;; </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3: [string, ...string[]]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4: string[]</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>The old behavior is now better represented with <code>z.tuple()</code> and a &quot;rest&quot; argument. This aligns more closely to TypeScript&#x27;s type system.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">tuple</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()], z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; [string, ...string[]]</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zpromise-deprecated"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zpromise-deprecated"><code>z.promise()</code> deprecated</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>There&#x27;s rarely a reason to use <code>z.promise()</code>. If you have an input that may be a <code>Promise</code>, just <code>await</code> it before parsing it with Zod.</p>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p>If you are using <code>z.promise</code> to define an async function with <code>z.function()</code>, that&#x27;s no longer necessary either; see the <a href="#function"><code>ZodFunction</code></a> section below.</p>
</div></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zfunction"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zfunction"><code>z.function()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The result of <code>z.function()</code> is no longer a Zod schema. Instead, it acts as a standalone &quot;function factory&quot; for defining Zod-validated functions. The API has also changed; you define an <code>input</code> and <code>output</code> schema upfront, instead of using <code>args()</code> and <code>.returns()</code> methods.</p>
<div dir="ltr" data-orientation="horizontal" class="flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-xl border bg-fd-card my-4"><div role="tablist" aria-orientation="horizontal" class="flex flex-row items-end dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> myFunction</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  input: [z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    age: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  })],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">myFunction.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">implement</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">((</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> `Hello ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">}, you are ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">age</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">} years old.`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_74iilubv9fl5b_-trigger-zod-3" hidden="" id="radix-_R_74iilubv9fl5b_-content-zod-3" tabindex="0" class="p-4 prose-no-margin [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:-m-4 [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:rounded-none [&amp;&gt;figure:only-child]:border-none"></div></div>
<p>If you have a desperate need for a Zod schema with a function type, consider <a href="https://github.com/colinhacks/zod/issues/4143#issuecomment-2845134912" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">this workaround</a>.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="adds-implementasync"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=adds-implementasync">adds <code>.implementAsync()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>To define an async function, use <code>implementAsync()</code> instead of <code>implement()</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">myFunction.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">implementAsync</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> `Hello ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">}, you are ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">age</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">} years old.`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="refine"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=refine"><code>.refine()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="ignores-type-predicates"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=ignores-type-predicates">ignores type predicates</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>In Zod 3, passing a <a href="https://www.typescriptlang.org/docs/handbook/2/narrowing.html#using-type-predicates" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">type predicate</a> as a refinement functions could still narrow the type of a schema. This wasn&#x27;t documented but was discussed in some issues. This is no longer the case.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> mySchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">val</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70"> val</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> is</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> typeof</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> val </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">===</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;string&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> MySchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">infer</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">typeof</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> mySchema&gt;; </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3: `string`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4: still `unknown`</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-ctxpath"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-ctxpath">drops <code>ctx.path</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Zod&#x27;s new parsing architecture does not eagerly evaluate the <code>path</code> array. This was a necessary change that unlocks Zod 4&#x27;s dramatic performance improvements.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  ctx.path; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ no longer available</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-function-as-second-argument"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-function-as-second-argument">drops function as second argument</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The following horrifying overload has been removed.</p>

[@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 longString</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span
