<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">val</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> ({ message: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">`${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">val</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">} is not more than 10 characters`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> })</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<!-- -->
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zostring-etc-dropped"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zostring-etc-dropped"><code>z.ostring()</code>, etc dropped</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>The undocumented convenience methods <code>z.ostring()</code>, <code>z.onumber()</code>, etc. have been removed. These were shorthand methods for defining optional string schemas.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zliteral"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zliteral"><code>z.literal()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-symbol-support"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-symbol-support">drops <code>symbol</code> support</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Symbols aren&#x27;t considered literal values, nor can they be simply compared with <code>===</code>. This was an oversight in Zod 3.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="static-create-factories-dropped"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=static-create-factories-dropped">static <code>.create()</code> factories dropped</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Previously all Zod classes defined a static <code>.create()</code> method. These are now implemented as standalone factory functions.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.ZodString.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">create</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ </span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zrecord"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zrecord"><code>z.record()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-single-argument-usage"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-single-argument-usage">drops single argument usage</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Before, <code>z.record()</code> could be used with a single argument. This is no longer supported.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">record</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">record</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">record</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(), z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="improves-enum-support"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=improves-enum-support">improves enum support</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Records have gotten a lot smarter. In Zod 3, passing an enum into <code>z.record()</code> as a key schema would result in a partial type</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> myRecord</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">record</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">enum</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">([</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;a&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;b&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;c&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">]), z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// { a?: number; b?: number; c?: number; }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>In Zod 4, this is no longer the case. The inferred type is what you&#x27;d expect, and Zod ensures exhaustiveness; that is, it makes sure all enum keys exist in the input during parsing.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> myRecord</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// { a: number; b: number; c: number; }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>To replicate the old behavior with optional keys, use <code>z.partialRecord()</code>:</p>

data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// { a?: number; b?: number; c?: number; }</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="zintersection"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=zintersection"><code>z.intersection()</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="throws-error-on-merge-conflict"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=throws-error-on-merge-conflict">throws <code>Error</code> on merge conflict</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Zod intersection parses the input against two schemas, then attempts to merge the results. In Zod 3, when the results were unmergable, Zod threw a <code>ZodError</code> with a special <code>&quot;invalid_intersection_types&quot;</code> issue.</p>
<p>In Zod 4, this will throw a regular <code>Error</code> instead. The existence of unmergable results indicates a structural problem with the schema: an intersection of two incompatible types. Thus, a regular error is more appropriate than a validation error.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="internal-changes"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=internal-changes">Internal changes</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p>The typical user of Zod can likely ignore everything below this line. These changes do not impact the user-facing <code>z</code> APIs.</p>
</div></div></div>
<p>There are too many internal changes to list here, but some may be relevant to regular users who are (intentionally or not) relying on certain implementation details. These changes will be of particular interest to library authors building tools on top of Zod.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="updates-generics"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=updates-generics">updates generics</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The generic structure of several classes has changed. Perhaps most significant is the change to the <code>ZodType</code> base class:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 3</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">class</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Output</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Def</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">ZodTypeDef</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Output</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">class</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Output</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">Input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>The second generic <code>Def</code> has been entirely removed. Instead the base class now only tracks <code>Output</code> and <code>Input</code>. While previously the <code>Input</code> value defaulted to <code>Output</code>, it now defaults to <code>unknown</code>. This allows generic functions involving <code>z.ZodType</code> to behave more intuitively in many cases.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> schema;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">};</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// z.ZodString</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>The need for <code>z.ZodTypeAny</code> has been eliminated; just use <code>z.ZodType</code> instead.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="adds-zcore"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=adds-zcore">adds <code>z.core</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Many utility functions and types have been moved to the new <code>zod/v4/core</code> sub-package, to facilitate code sharing between Zod and Zod Mini.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 <span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> handleError</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">iss</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodError</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>For convenience, the contents of <code>zod/v4/core</code> are also re-exported from <code>zod</code> and <code>zod/mini</code> under the <code>z.core</code> namespace.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 <span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> handleError</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">iss</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">core</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodError</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // do stuff</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Refer to the <a href="/packages/core">Zod Core</a> docs for more information on the contents of the core sub-library.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="moves-_def"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=moves-_def">moves <code>._def</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>The <code>._def</code> property is now moved to <code>._zod.def</code>. The structure of all internal defs is subject to change; this is relevant to library authors but won&#x27;t be comprehensively documented here.</p>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-zodeffects"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-zodeffects">drops <code>ZodEffects</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>This doesn&#x27;t affect the user-facing APIs, but it&#x27;s an internal change worth highlighting. It&#x27;s part of a larger restructure of how Zod handles <em>refinements</em>.</p>
<p>Previously both refinements and transformations lived inside a wrapper class called <code>ZodEffects</code>. That means adding either one to a schema would wrap the original schema in a <code>ZodEffects</code> instance. In Zod 4, refinements now live inside the schemas themselves. More accurately, each schema contains an array of &quot;checks&quot;; the concept of a &quot;check&quot; is new in Zod 4 and generalizes the concept of a refinement to include potentially side-effectful transforms like <code>z.toLowerCase()</code>.</p>
<p>This is particularly apparent in the Zod Mini API, which heavily relies on the <code>.check()</code> method to compose various validations together.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/mini&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">check</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">minLength</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">maxLength</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">100</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">toLowerCase</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">trim</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="adds-zodtransform"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=adds-zodtransform">adds <code>ZodTransform</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Meanwhile, transforms have been moved into a dedicated <code>ZodTransform</code> class. This schema class represents an input transform; in fact, you can actually define standalone transformations now:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span <span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">transform</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">input</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> String</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(input));</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">schema.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">12</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; &quot;12&quot;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>This is primarily used in conjunction with <code>ZodPipe</code>. The <code>.transform()</code> method now returns an instance of <code>ZodPipe</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" ZodTransform&gt;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-zodpreprocess"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-zodpreprocess">drops <code>ZodPreprocess</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>As with <code>.transform()</code>, the <code>z.preprocess()</code> function now returns a <code>ZodPipe</code> instance instead of a dedicated <code>ZodPreprocess</code> instance.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">preprocess</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">val</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> val, z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ZodPipe&lt;ZodTransform, ZodString&gt;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h3 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="drops-zodbranded"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=drops-zodbranded">drops <code>ZodBranded</code></a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h3>
<p>Branding is now handled with a direct modification to the inferred type, instead of a dedicated <code>ZodBranded</code> class. The user-facing APIs remain the same.</p>

guide\n\nimport { Callout } from \"fumadocs-ui/components/callout\";\nimport { Tabs, Tab } from \"fumadocs-ui/components/tabs\";\n\nThis migration guide aims to list the breaking changes in Zod 4 in order of highest to lowest impact. To learn more about the performance enhancements and new features of Zod 4, read the [introductory post](/v4).\n\n{/* To give the ecosystem time to migrate, Zod 4 will initially be published alongside Zod v3.25. To use Zod 4, upgrade to `zod@3.25.0` or later: */}\n\n```\nnpm install zod@^4.0.0\n```\n\n{/* Zod 4 is available at the `\"/v4\"` subpath:\n\n  ```ts\n  import * as z from \"zod\";\n  ``` */}\n\nMany of Zod's behaviors and APIs have been made more intuitive and cohesive. The breaking changes described in this document often represent major quality-of-life improvements for Zod users. I strongly recommend reading this guide thoroughly.\n\n\u003cCallout\u003e\n  **Note** — Zod 3 exported a number of undocumented quasi-internal utility types and functions that are not considered part of the public API. Changes to those are not documented here.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\n\u003cCallout\u003e\n  **Unofficial codemod** — A community-maintained codemod [`zod-v3-to-v4`](https://github.com/nicoespeon/zod-v3-to-v4) is available.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\n## Error customization\n\nZod 4 standardizes the APIs for error customization under a single, unified `error` param. Previously Zod's error customization APIs were fragmented and inconsistent. This is cleaned up in Zod 4.\n\n### deprecates `message` parameter\n\nReplaces `message` param with `error`. The old `message` parameter is still supported but deprecated.\n\n\u003cTabs groupId=\"error-message\" items={[\"Zod 4\", \"Zod 3\"]} persist\u003e\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod 4\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    z.string().min(5, { error: \"Too short.\" });\n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod 3\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    z.string().min(5, { message: \"Too short.\" });\n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs\u003e\n\n### drops `invalid_type_error` and `required_error`\n\nThe `invalid_type_error` / `required_error` params have been dropped. These were hastily added years ago as a way to customize errors that was less verbose than `errorMap`. They came with all sorts of footguns (they can't be used in conjunction with `errorMap`) and do not align with Zod's actual issue codes (there is no `required` issue code).\n\nThese can now be cleanly represented with the new `error` parameter.\n\n\u003cTabs groupId=\"error-type\" items={[\"Zod 4\", \"Zod 3\"]} persist\u003e\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod 4\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    z.string({ \n      error: (issue) =\u003e issue.input === undefined \n        ? \"This field is required\" \n        : \"Not a string\" \n    });\n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod 3\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    z.string({ \n      required_error: \"This field is required\",\n      invalid_type_error: \"Not a string\", \n    });\n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs\u003e\n\n### drops `errorMap`\n\nThis is renamed to `error`.\n\nError maps can also now return a plain `string` (instead of `{message: string}`). They can also return `undefined`, which tells Zod to yield control to the next error map in the chain.\n\n\u003cTabs groupId=\"error-map\" items={[\"Zod 4\", \"Zod 3\"]} persist\u003e\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod 4\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    z.string().min(5, {\n      error: (issue) =\u003e {\n        if (issue.code === \"too_small\") {\n          return `Value must be \u003e${issue.minimum}`\n        }\n      },\n    });\n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod 3\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    z.string({\n      errorMap: (issue, ctx) =\u003e {\n        if (issue.code === \"too_small\") {\n          return { message: `Value must be \u003e${issue.minimum}` };\n        }\n        return { message: ctx.defaultError };\n      },\n    });\n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs\u003e\n\n{/* ## `.safeParse()` \n\n  For performance reasons, the errors returned by `.safeParse()` and `.safeParseAsync()` no longer extend `Error`. \n\n  ```ts\n  const result = z.string().safeParse(12); \n  result.error! instanceof Error; // =\u003e false\n  ```\n\n  It is very slow to instantiate `Error` instances in JavaScript, as the initialization process snapshots the call stack. In the case of Zod's \"safe\" parse methods, it's expected that you will handle errors at the point of parsing, so instantiating a true `Error` object adds little value anyway. \n\n  \u003e Pro tip: prefer `.safeParse()` over `try/catch` in performance-sensitive code.\n\n  By contrast the errors thrown by `.parse()` and `.parseAsync()` still extend `Error`. Aside from the prototype difference, the error classes are identical.\n\n  ```ts\n  try {\n  z.string().parse(12);\n  } catch (err) {\n  console.log(err instanceof Error); // =\u003e true\n  }\n  ```\n  */}\n\n## `ZodError`\n\n{/* \n  ### changes to `.message` \n\n  Previously the `.message` property on `ZodError` was a JSON.stringified copy of the `.issues` array. This was redundant, confusing, and a bit of an abuse of the `.message` property. Also due to the [`Error` prototype changes](#safeparse) (and inconsistencies in how Node.js logs `Error` subclasses vs other objects) the logging of a multi-line `.message` property got a lot uglier:\n\n  ```sh\n  $ tsx index.ts\n  ZodError {\n  message: '[\\n' +\n    '  {\\n' +\n    '    \"expected\": \"string\",\\n' +\n    '    \"code\": \"invalid_type\",\\n' +\n    '    \"path\": [],\\n' +\n    '    \"message\": \"Invalid input: expected string, received number\"\\n' +\n    '  }\\n' +\n    ']'\n  }\n  ```\n\n\n  For these reasons, the `.message` property is left empty and the `.issues` array is marked as enumerable. This keeps error logging consistent and pretty:\n\n  ```sh\n  $ tsx index.ts\n  z.string().parse(234);\n\n  ZodError {\n  issues: [\n    {\n      expected: 'string',\n      code: 'invalid_type',\n      path: [],\n      message: 'Invalid input: expected string, received number'\n    }\n  ]\n  }\n  ```\n\n  Vitest uses special handling for `Error` subclasses that ignores enumerable properties.  */}\n\n### updates issue formats\n\nThe issue formats have been dramatically streamlined.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\"; // v4\n\ntype IssueFormats = \n  | z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidType\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueTooBig\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueTooSmall\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidStringFormat\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueNotMultipleOf\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueUnrecognizedKeys\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidValue\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidUnion\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidKey // new: used for z.record/z.map \n  | z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidElement // new: used for z.map/z.set\n  | z.core.$ZodIssueCustom;\n```\n\nBelow is the list of Zod 3 issues types and their Zod 4 equivalent:\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\"; // v3\n\nexport type IssueFormats =\n  | z.ZodInvalidTypeIssue // ♻️ renamed to z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidType\n  | z.ZodTooBigIssue  // ♻️ renamed to z.core.$ZodIssueTooBig\n  | z.ZodTooSmallIssue // ♻️ renamed to z.core.$ZodIssueTooSmall\n  | z.ZodInvalidStringIssue // ♻️ z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidStringFormat\n  | z.ZodNotMultipleOfIssue // ♻️ renamed to z.core.$ZodIssueNotMultipleOf\n  | z.ZodUnrecognizedKeysIssue // ♻️ renamed to z.core.$ZodIssueUnrecognizedKeys\n  | z.ZodInvalidUnionIssue // ♻️ renamed to z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidUnion\n  | z.ZodCustomIssue // ♻️ renamed to z.core.$ZodIssueCustom\n  | z.ZodInvalidEnumValueIssue // ❌ merged in z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidValue\n  | z.ZodInvalidLiteralIssue // ❌ merged into z.core.$ZodIssueInvalidValue\n  | z.ZodInvalidUnionDiscriminatorIssue // ❌ throws an Error at schema creation time\n  | z.ZodInvalidArgumentsIssue // ❌ z.function throws ZodError directly\n  | z.ZodInvalidReturnTypeIssue // ❌ z.function throws ZodError directly\n  | z.ZodInvalidDateIssue // ❌ merged into invalid_type\n  | z.ZodInvalidIntersectionTypesIssue // ❌ removed (throws regular Error)\n  | z.ZodNotFiniteIssue // ❌ infinite values no longer accepted (invalid_type)\n```\n\nWhile certain Zod 4 issue types have been merged, dropped, and modified, each issue remains structurally similar to Zod 3 counterpart (identical, in most cases). All issues still conform to the same base interface as Zod 3, so most common error handling logic will work without modification.\n\n```ts\nexport interface $ZodIssueBase {\n  readonly code?: string;\n  readonly input?: unknown;\n  readonly path: PropertyKey[];\n  readonly message: string;\n}\n```\n\n### changes error map precedence\n\nThe error map precedence has been changed to be more consistent. Specifically, an error map passed into `.parse()` *no longer* takes precedence over a schema-level error map.\n\n```ts\nconst mySchema = z.string({ error: () =\u003e \"Schema-level error\" });\n\n// in Zod 3\nmySchema.parse(12, { error: () =\u003e \"Contextual error\" }); // =\u003e \"Contextual error\"\n\n// in Zod 4\nmySchema.parse(12, { error: () =\u003e \"Contextual error\" }); // =\u003e \"Schema-level error\"\n```\n\n### deprecates `.format()`\n\nThe `.format()` method on `ZodError` has been deprecated. Instead use the top-level `z.treeifyError()` function. Read the [Formatting errors docs](/error-formatting) for more information.\n\n### deprecates `.flatten()`\n\nThe `.flatten()` method on `ZodError` has also been deprecated. Instead use the top-level `z.treeifyError()` function. Read the [Formatting errors docs](/error-formatting) for more information.\n\n### drops `.formErrors`\n\nThis API was identical to `.flatten()`. It exists for historical reasons and isn't documented.\n\n### deprecates `.addIssue()` and `.addIssues()`\n\nDirectly push to `err.issues` array instead, if necessary.\n\n```ts\nmyError.issues.push({ \n  // new issue\n});\n```\n\n{/* ## `.and()` dropped\n\n  The `.and()` method on `ZodType` has been dropped in favor of `z.intersection(A, B)`. Not only is this method rarely used, there are few good reasons to use intersections at all. The `.and()` API prevented bundlers from treeshaking `ZodIntersection`, a fairly large and complex class. \n\n  ```ts\n  z.object({ a: z.string() }).and(z.object({ b: z.number() })); // ❌\n\n  // use z.intersection\n  z.intersection(z.object({ a: z.string() }), z.object({ b: z.number() })); // ✅\n  // or .extend() when possible\n  z.object({ a: z.string() }).extend(z.object({ b: z.number() })); // ✅\n  ``` */}\n\n## `z.number()`\n\n### no infinite values\n\n`POSITIVE_INFINITY` and `NEGATIVE_INFINITY` are no longer considered valid values for `z.number()`.\n\n### `.safe()` no longer accepts floats\n\nIn Zod 3, `z.number().safe()` is deprecated. It now behaves identically to `.int()` (see below). Importantly, that means it no longer accepts floats.\n\n### `.int()` accepts safe integers only\n\nThe `z.number().int()` API no longer accepts unsafe integers (outside the range of `Number.MIN_SAFE_INTEGER` and `Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER`). Using integers out of this range causes spontaneous rounding errors. (Also: You should switch to `z.int()`.)\n\n## `z.string()` updates\n\n### deprecates `.email()` etc\n\nString formats are now represented as *subclasses* of `ZodString`, instead of simple internal refinements. As such, these APIs have been moved to the top-level `z` namespace. Top-level APIs are also less verbose and more tree-shakable.\n\n```ts\nz.email();\nz.uuid();\nz.url();\nz.emoji();         // validates a single emoji character\nz.base64();\nz.base64url();\nz.nanoid();\nz.cuid();\nz.cuid2();\nz.ulid();\nz.ipv4();\nz.ipv6();\nz.cidrv4();          // ip range\nz.cidrv6();          // ip range\nz.iso.date();\nz.iso.time();\nz.iso.datetime();\nz.iso.duration();\n```\n\nThe method forms (`z.string().email()`) still exist and work as before, but are now deprecated.\n\n```ts\nz.string().email(); // ❌ deprecated\nz.email(); // ✅ \n```\n\n### stricter `.uuid()`\n\nThe `z.uuid()` now validates UUIDs more strictly against the RFC 9562/4122 specification; specifically, the variant bits must be `10` per the spec. For a more permissive \"UUID-like\" validator, use `z.guid()`.\n\n```ts\nz.uuid(); // RFC 9562/4122 compliant UUID\nz.guid(); // any 8-4-4-4-12 hex pattern\n```\n\n### no padding in `.base64url()`\n\nPadding is no longer allowed in `z.base64url()` (formerly `z.string().base64url()`). Generally it's desirable for base64url strings to be unpadded and URL-safe.\n\n### drops `z.string().ip()`\n\nThis has been replaced with separate `.ipv4()` and `.ipv6()` methods. Use `z.union()` to combine them if you need to accept both.\n\n```ts\nz.string().ip() // ❌\nz.ipv4() // ✅\nz.ipv6() // ✅\n```\n\n### updates `z.string().ipv6()`\n\nValidation now happens using the `new URL()` constructor, which is far more robust than the old regular expression approach. Some invalid values that passed validation previously may now fail.\n\n### drops `z.string().cidr()`\n\nSimilarly, this has been replaced with separate `.cidrv4()` and `.cidrv6()` methods. Use `z.union()` to combine them if you need to accept both.\n\n```ts\nz.string().cidr() // ❌\nz.cidrv4() // ✅\nz.cidrv6() // ✅\n```\n\n## `z.coerce` updates\n\nThe input type of all `z.coerce` schemas is now `unknown`.\n\n```ts\nconst schema = z.coerce.string();\ntype schemaInput = z.input\u003ctypeof schema\u003e;\n\n// Zod 3: string;\n// Zod 4: unknown;\n```\n\n## `.default()` updates\n\nThe application of `.default()` has changed in a subtle way. If the input is `undefined`, `ZodDefault` short-circuits the parsing process and returns the default value. The default value must be assignable to the *output type*.\n\n```ts\nconst schema = z.string()\n  .transform(val =\u003e val.length)\n  .default(0); // should be a number\nschema.parse(undefined); // =\u003e 0\n```\n\nIn Zod 3, `.default()` expected a value that matched the *input type*. `ZodDefault` would parse the default value, instead of short-circuiting. As such, the default value must be assignable to the *input type* of the schema.\n\n```ts\n// Zod 3\nconst schema = z.string()\n  .transform(val =\u003e val.length)\n  .default(\"tuna\");\nschema.parse(undefined); // =\u003e 4\n```\n\nTo replicate the old behavior, Zod implements a new `.prefault()` API. This is short for \"pre-parse default\".\n\n```ts\n// Zod 3\nconst schema = z.string()\n  .transform(val =\u003e val.length)\n  .prefault(\"tuna\");\nschema.parse(undefined); // =\u003e 4\n```\n\n## `z.object()`\n\n### defaults applied within optional fields\n\nDefaults inside your properties are applied, even within optional fields. This aligns better with expectations and resolves a long-standing usability issue with Zod 3. This is a subtle change that may cause breakage in code paths that rely on key existence, etc.\n\n```ts\nconst schema = z.object({\n  a: z.string().default(\"tuna\").optional(),\n});\n\nschema.parse({});\n// Zod 4: { a: \"tuna\" }\n// Zod 3: {}\n```\n\n### deprecates `.strict()` and `.passthrough()`\n\nThese methods are generally no longer necessary. Instead use the top-level `z.strictObject()` and `z.looseObject()` functions.\n\n```ts\n// Zod 3\nz.object({ name: z.string() }).strict();\nz.object({ name: z.string() }).passthrough();\n\n// Zod 4\nz.strictObject({ name: z.string() });\nz.looseObject({ name: z.string() });\n```\n\n\u003e These methods are still available for backwards compatibility, and they will not be removed. They are considered legacy.\n\n### deprecates `.strip()`\n\nThis was never particularly useful, as it was the default behavior of `z.object()`. To convert a strict object to a \"regular\" one, use `z.object(A.shape)`.\n\n### drops `.nonstrict()`\n\nThis long-deprecated alias for `.strip()` has been removed.\n\n### drops `.deepPartial()`\n\nThis has been long deprecated in Zod 3 and it now removed in Zod 4. There is no direct alternative to this API. There were lots of footguns in its implementation, and its use is generally an anti-pattern.\n\n### changes `z.unknown()` optionality\n\nThe `z.unknown()` and `z.any()` types are no longer marked as \"key optional\" in the inferred types.\n\n```ts\nconst mySchema = z.object({\n  a: z.any(),\n  b: z.unknown()\n});\n// Zod 3: { a?: any; b?: unknown };\n// Zod 4: { a: any; b: unknown };\n```\n\n### deprecates `.merge()`\n\nThe `.merge()` method on `ZodObject` has been deprecated in favor of `.extend()`. The `.extend()` method provides the same functionality, avoids ambiguity around strictness inheritance, and has better TypeScript performance.\n\n```ts\n// .merge (deprecated)\nconst ExtendedSchema = BaseSchema.merge(AdditionalSchema);\n\n// .extend (recommended)\nconst ExtendedSchema = BaseSchema.extend(AdditionalSchema.shape);\n\n// or use destructuring (best tsc performance)\nconst ExtendedSchema = z.object({\n  ...BaseSchema.shape,\n  ...AdditionalSchema.shape,\n});\n```\n\n\u003e **Note**: For even better TypeScript performance, consider using object destructuring instead of `.extend()`. See the [API documentation](/api?id=extend) for more details.\n\n## `z.nativeEnum()` deprecated\n\nThe `z.nativeEnum()` function is now deprecated in favor of just `z.enum()`. The `z.enum()` API has been overloaded to support an enum-like input.\n\n```ts\nenum Color {\n  Red = \"red\",\n  Green = \"green\",\n  Blue = \"blue\",\n}\n\nconst ColorSchema = z.enum(Color); // ✅\n```\n\nAs part of this refactor of `ZodEnum`, a number of long-deprecated and redundant features have been removed. These were all identical and only existed for historical reasons.\n\n```ts\nColorSchema.enum.Red; // ✅ =\u003e \"Red\" (canonical API)\nColorSchema.Enum.Red; // ❌ removed\nColorSchema.Values.Red; // ❌ removed\n```\n\n## `z.array()`\n\n### changes `.nonempty()` type\n\nThis now behaves identically to `z.array().min(1)`. The inferred type does not change.\n\n```ts\nconst NonEmpty = z.array(z.string()).nonempty();\n\ntype NonEmpty = z.infer\u003ctypeof NonEmpty\u003e; \n// Zod 3: [string, ...string[]]\n// Zod 4: string[]\n```\n\nThe old behavior is now better represented with `z.tuple()` and a \"rest\" argument. This aligns more closely to TypeScript's type system.\n\n```ts\nz.tuple([z.string()], z.string());\n// =\u003e [string, ...string[]]\n```\n\n## `z.promise()` deprecated\n\nThere's rarely a reason to use `z.promise()`. If you have an input that may be a `Promise`, just `await` it before parsing it with Zod.\n\n\u003e If you are using `z.promise` to define an async function with `z.function()`, that's no longer necessary either; see the [`ZodFunction`](#function) section below.\n\n## `z.function()`\n\nThe result of `z.function()` is no longer a Zod schema. Instead, it acts as a standalone \"function factory\" for defining Zod-validated functions. The API has also changed; you define an `input` and `output` schema upfront, instead of using `args()` and `.returns()` methods.\n\n\u003cTabs groupId=\"lib\" items={[\"Zod 4\", \"Zod 3\"]} persist\u003e\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod 4\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    const myFunction = z.function({\n      input: [z.object({\n        name: z.string(),\n        age: z.number().int(),\n      })],\n      output: z.string(),\n    });\n\n    myFunction.implement((input) =\u003e {\n      return `Hello ${input.name}, you are ${input.age} years old.`;\n    });\n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\n  \u003cTab value=\"Zod 3\"\u003e\n    ```ts\n    const myFunction = z.function()\n      .args(z.object({\n        name: z.string(),\n        age: z.number().int(),\n      }))\n      .returns(z.string());\n\n    myFunction.implement((input) =\u003e {\n      return `Hello ${input.name}, you are ${input.age} years old.`;\n    });\n    ```\n  \u003c/Tab\u003e\n\u003c/Tabs\u003e\n\nIf you have a desperate need for a Zod schema with a function type, consider [this workaround](https://github.com/colinhacks/zod/issues/4143#issuecomment-2845134912).\n\n### adds `.implementAsync()`\n\nTo define an async function, use `implementAsync()` instead of `implement()`.\n\n```ts\nmyFunction.implementAsync(async (input) =\u003e {\n  return `Hello ${input.name}, you are ${input.age} years old.`;\n});\n```\n\n## `.refine()`\n\n### ignores type predicates\n\nIn Zod 3, passing a [type predicate](https://www.typescriptlang.org/docs/handbook/2/narrowing.html#using-type-predicates) as a refinement functions could still narrow the type of a schema. This wasn't documented but was discussed in some issues. This is no longer the case.\n\n```ts\nconst mySchema = z.unknown().refine((val): val is string =\u003e {\n  return typeof val === \"string\"\n});\n\ntype MySchema = z.infer\u003ctypeof mySchema\u003e; \n// Zod 3: `string`\n// Zod 4: still `unknown`\n```\n\n### drops `ctx.path`\n\nZod's new parsing architecture does not eagerly evaluate the `path` array. This was a necessary change that unlocks Zod 4's dramatic performance improvements.\n\n```ts\nz.string().superRefine((val, ctx) =\u003e {\n  ctx.path; // ❌ no longer available\n});\n```\n\n### drops function as second argument\n\nThe following horrifying overload has been removed.\n\n```ts\nconst longString = z.string().refine(\n  (val) =\u003e val.length \u003e 10,\n  (val) =\u003e ({ message: `${val} is not more than 10 characters` })\n);\n```\n\n{/* ## `.superRefine()` deprecated\n\n  The `.superRefine()` method has been deprecated in favor of `.check()`. The `.check()` method provides the same functionality with a cleaner API. The `.check()` method is also available on Zod and Zod Mini schemas.\n\n  ```ts\n  const UniqueStringArray = z.array(z.string()).check((ctx) =\u003e {\n  if (ctx.value.length \u003e 3) {\n    ctx.issues.push({\n      code: \"too_big\",\n      maximum: 3,\n      origin: \"array\",\n      inclusive: true,\n      message: \"Too many items 😡\",\n      input: ctx.value\n    });\n  }\n\n  if (ctx.value.length !== new Set(ctx.value).size) {\n    ctx.issues.push({\n      code: \"custom\",\n      message: `No duplicates allowed.`,\n      input: ctx.value\n    });\n  }\n  });\n  ``` */}\n\n## `z.ostring()`, etc dropped\n\nThe undocumented convenience methods `z.ostring()`, `z.onumber()`, etc. have been removed. These were shorthand methods for defining optional string schemas.\n\n## `z.literal()`\n\n### drops `symbol` support\n\nSymbols aren't considered literal values, nor can they be simply compared with `===`. This was an oversight in Zod 3.\n\n## static `.create()` factories dropped\n\nPreviously all Zod classes defined a static `.create()` method. These are now implemented as standalone factory functions.\n\n```ts\nz.ZodString.create(); // ❌ \n```\n\n## `z.record()`\n\n### drops single argument usage\n\nBefore, `z.record()` could be used with a single argument. This is no longer supported.\n\n```ts\n// Zod 3\nz.record(z.string()); // ✅\n\n// Zod 4\nz.record(z.string()); // ❌\nz.record(z.string(), z.string()); // ✅\n```\n\n### improves enum support\n\nRecords have gotten a lot smarter. In Zod 3, passing an enum into `z.record()` as a key schema would result in a partial type\n\n```ts\nconst myRecord = z.record(z.enum([\"a\", \"b\", \"c\"]), z.number()); \n// { a?: number; b?: number; c?: number; }\n```\n\nIn Zod 4, this is no longer the case. The inferred type is what you'd expect, and Zod ensures exhaustiveness; that is, it makes sure all enum keys exist in the input during parsing.\n\n```ts\nconst myRecord = z.record(z.enum([\"a\", \"b\", \"c\"]), z.number());\n// { a: number; b: number; c: number; }\n```\n\nTo replicate the old behavior with optional keys, use `z.partialRecord()`:\n\n```ts\nconst myRecord = z.partialRecord(z.enum([\"a\", \"b\", \"c\"]), z.number());\n// { a?: number; b?: number; c?: number; }\n```\n\n## `z.intersection()`\n\n### throws `Error` on merge conflict\n\nZod intersection parses the input against two schemas, then attempts to merge the results. In Zod 3, when the results were unmergable, Zod threw a `ZodError` with a special `\"invalid_intersection_types\"` issue.\n\nIn Zod 4, this will throw a regular `Error` instead. The existence of unmergable results indicates a structural problem with the schema: an intersection of two incompatible types. Thus, a regular error is more appropriate than a validation error.\n\n## Internal changes\n\n\u003e The typical user of Zod can likely ignore everything below this line. These changes do not impact the user-facing `z` APIs.\n\nThere are too many internal changes to list here, but some may be relevant to regular users who are (intentionally or not) relying on certain implementation details. These changes will be of particular interest to library authors building tools on top of Zod.\n\n### updates generics\n\nThe generic structure of several classes has changed. Perhaps most significant is the change to the `ZodType` base class:\n\n```ts\n// Zod 3\nclass ZodType\u003cOutput, Def extends z.ZodTypeDef, Input = Output\u003e {\n  // ...\n}\n\n// Zod 4\nclass ZodType\u003cOutput = unknown, Input = unknown\u003e {\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\nThe second generic `Def` has been entirely removed. Instead the base class now only tracks `Output` and `Input`. While previously the `Input` value defaulted to `Output`, it now defaults to `unknown`. This allows generic functions involving `z.ZodType` to behave more intuitively in many cases.\n\n```ts\nfunction inferSchema\u003cT extends z.ZodType\u003e(schema: T): T {\n  return schema;\n};\n\ninferSchema(z.string()); // z.ZodString\n```\n\nThe need for `z.ZodTypeAny` has been eliminated; just use `z.ZodType` instead.\n\n### adds `z.core`\n\nMany utility functions and types have been moved to the new `zod/v4/core` sub-package, to facilitate code sharing between Zod and Zod Mini.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\nfunction handleError(iss: z.$ZodError) {\n  // do stuff\n}\n```\n\nFor convenience, the contents of `zod/v4/core` are also re-exported from `zod` and `zod/mini` under the `z.core` namespace.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\";\n\nfunction handleError(iss: z.core.$ZodError) {\n  // do stuff\n}\n```\n\nRefer to the [Zod Core](/packages/core) docs for more information on the contents of the core sub-library.\n\n### moves `._def`\n\nThe `._def` property is now moved to `._zod.def`. The structure of all internal defs is subject to change; this is relevant to library authors but won't be comprehensively documented here.\n\n### drops `ZodEffects`\n\nThis doesn't affect the user-facing APIs, but it's an internal change worth highlighting. It's part of a larger restructure of how Zod handles *refinements*.\n\nPreviously both refinements and transformations lived inside a wrapper class called `ZodEffects`. That means adding either one to a schema would wrap the original schema in a `ZodEffects` instance. In Zod 4, refinements now live inside the schemas themselves. More accurately, each schema contains an array of \"checks\"; the concept of a \"check\" is new in Zod 4 and generalizes the concept of a refinement to include potentially side-effectful transforms like `z.toLowerCase()`.\n\nThis is particularly apparent in the Zod Mini API, which heavily relies on the `.check()` method to compose various validations together.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod/mini\";\n\nz.string().check(\n  z.minLength(10),\n  z.maxLength(100),\n  z.toLowerCase(),\n  z.trim(),\n);\n```\n\n### adds `ZodTransform`\n\nMeanwhile, transforms have been moved into a dedicated `ZodTransform` class. This schema class represents an input transform; in fact, you can actually define standalone transformations now:\n\n```ts\nimport * as z from \"zod\";\n\nconst schema = z.transform(input =\u003e String(input));\n\nschema.parse(12); // =\u003e \"12\"\n```\n\nThis is primarily used in conjunction with `ZodPipe`. The `.transform()` method now returns an instance of `ZodPipe`.\n\n```ts\nz.string().transform(val =\u003e val); // ZodPipe\u003cZodString, ZodTransform\u003e\n```\n\n### drops `ZodPreprocess`\n\nAs with `.transform()`, the `z.preprocess()` function now returns a `ZodPipe` instance instead of a dedicated `ZodPreprocess` instance.\n\n```ts\nz.preprocess(val =\u003e val, z.string()); // ZodPipe\u003cZodTransform, ZodString\u003e\n```\n\n### drops `ZodBranded`\n\nBranding is now handled with a direct modification to the inferred type, instead of a dedicated `ZodBranded` class. The user-facing APIs remain the same.\n\n{/* - Dropping support for ES5\n  - Zod relies on `Set` internally */}\n\n{/* - `z.keyof` now returns `ZodEnum` instead of `ZodLiteral` */}\n\n{/* ## Changed: `.refine()`\n\n  The `.refine()` method used to accept a function as the second argument. \n\n  ```ts\n  // no longer supported\n  const longString = z.string().refine(\n  (val) =\u003e val.length \u003e 10,\n  (val) =\u003e ({ message: `${val} is not more than 10 characters` })\n  );\n  ```\n\n  This can be better represented with the new `error` parameter, so this overload has been removed.\n\n  ```ts\n  const longString = z.string().refine((val) =\u003e val.length \u003e 10, {\n  error: (issue) =\u003e `${issue.input} is not more than 10 characters`,\n  });\n  ``\n  */}\n\n{/* \n  - No support for `null` or `undefined` in `z.literal`\n  - `z.literal(null)`\n  - `z.literal(undefined)`\n  - this was never documented */}\n\n{/* - Array min/max/length checks now run after parsing. This means they won't run if the parse has already aborted. */}\n\n{/* - Drops single-argument `z.record()` */}\n\n{/* - Smarter `z.record`: no longer Partial by default */}\n\n{/* - Intersection merge errors are now thrown as Error not ZodError\n  - These usually do not reflect a parse error but a structural problem with the schema */}\n\n{/* - Consolidates `unknownKeys` and `catchall` in ZodObject */}\n\n{/* - Dropping\n  - `ZodBranded`: purely a static-domain annotation\n  - `ZodFunction` */}\n\n{/* - The `description` is now stored in `z.defaultRegistry`, not the def\n  - No support for `description` in factory params\n  - Descriptions do not cascade in `.optional()`, etc */}\n\n{/* - Enums:\n  - ZodEnum and ZodNativeEnum are merged\n  - `.Values` and `.Enum` are removed. Use `.enum` instead.\n  - `.options` is removed */}\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"42:[\"$\",\"$L44\",null,{\"className\":\"\",\"style\":{\"--fd-tocnav-height\":\"$undefined\"},\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L45\",null,{\"className\":\"h-10\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L46\",null,{\"className\":\"w-full\",\"items\":\"$26:props:toc\"}],[\"$\",\"$L47\",null,{\"children\":[\"$undefined\",[\"$\",\"$L48\",null,{\"isMenu\":true,\"children\":[\"$\",\"$L49\",null,{\"items\":\"$26:props:toc\"}]}],\"$undefined\"]}]]}],[\"$\",\"$L4a\",null,{\"className\":\"max-w-[860px]\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L4b\",null,{}],[[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"mb-6\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"h1\",null,{\"ref\":\"$undefined\",\"children\":\"Migration
